#exp_behavior

behavior find_food_sugar_2070_around_fridge_140(food_sugar:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_sugar)
    body:
        assert is_food_sugar(food_sugar)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==140
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)
            exp(food_sugar,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_sugar,fridge_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_sugar]=False
        close[food_sugar,fridge_instance]=True
        close[fridge_instance,food_sugar]=True

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_in_trashcan(item:item, fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        observe(fridge, "Check items inside the fridge")
        # Observe items inside the fridge
        achieve_once inside(item, fridge)
        # This is redundant as observe will check, ensure item inside fridge
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
        # Throw the item into the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select fridge and trashcan
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                # Check all items in the fridge
                throw_items_in_trashcan(item, fridge, trashcan)
                # Throw them all in the trashcan

#goal_representation_end

#exp_behavior

#goal_representation
 
def is_in_fridge(item:item):
    # Function to check if an item is in the fridge
    symbol in_fridge = exists fridge: item : (is_fridge(fridge) and inside(item, fridge))
    return in_fridge

behavior throw_item_away(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan
        foreach item: item:
            if not is_in_fridge(item):
                achieve_once inside(item, fridge)
        # Move all items from the fridge to the trashcan
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_away(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

behavior find_food_sugar_2070_around_fridge_140(food_sugar:item):

            exp(food_sugar,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_sugar,fridge_instance)

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior move_items_to_trashcan(item_from_fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item_from_fridge, trashcan)
        # Move the item from the fridge to the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        foreach item_from_fridge: item:
            if inside(item_from_fridge, fridge):
                move_items_to_trashcan(item_from_fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item_to_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan) # Move the item to the inside of the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_to_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

    goal: not unknown(food_sugar)
    body:
        assert is_food_sugar(food_sugar)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==140
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)
            exp(food_sugar,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_sugar,fridge_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_sugar]=False

        close[fridge_instance,food_sugar]=True

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_in_trash(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan

        throw_items_in_trash(fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_in_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                bind trashcan: item where:
                    is_trashcan(trashcan)
                throw_in_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_away_items_from_fridge(fridge:item, trashcan:item, item_in_fridge:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item_in_fridge, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trash can

        foreach item_in_fridge: item:
            if inside(item_in_fridge, fridge):
                throw_away_items_from_fridge(fridge, trashcan, item_in_fridge)

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
        # Place the item inside the trashcan

behavior throw_items_in_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_in_trash(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Bind the fridge instance

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Bind the trashcan instance

        throw_items_in_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge, trashcan)
        # Execute the behavior to throw all items in the fridge into the trashcan

#goal_representation_end

##############################

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_in_trash(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach o: item:
            if inside(o, fridge):
                achieve_once inside(o, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan
        throw_items_in_trash(fridge, trashcan)
        # Dispose of all items in the fridge into the trashcan

#goal_representation_end

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_from_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge:item, trashcan:item): 
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge) and grabbable(item):
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge to take items from
        
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan to throw items into

        throw_items_from_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior

behavior find_food_sugar_2070_around_fridge_140(food_sugar:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_sugar)
    body:
        assert is_food_sugar(food_sugar)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==140
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)
            exp(food_sugar,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_sugar,fridge_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_sugar]=False

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Find all items inside the fridge and throw them into the trashcan
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_in_trash(item, trashcan)

behavior find_food_sugar_2070_around_fridge_140(food_sugar:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_sugar)
    body:
        assert is_food_sugar(food_sugar)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==140
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation

behavior throw_item_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item): 
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_in_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
        # Place the item inside the trashcan

behavior throw_all_items_from_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        # Go through all items inside the fridge and throw them in the trashcan
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_in_trash(item, trashcan)
        
behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Identify a fridge
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Identify a trashcan
        throw_all_items_from_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_in_trash(fridge_item: item, trashcan: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(fridge_item, trashcan)
        # Place the fridge item inside the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge
        
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trash can
        
        foreach fridge_item: item:
            if inside(fridge_item, fridge):
                throw_in_trash(fridge_item, trashcan)
                # Throw each item from the fridge into the trash can

#goal_representation_end

Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_away_from_fridge(item: item, trashcan: item, fridge: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
        # Move item from the fridge to the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select a trashcan
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                # Check all items in the fridge
                throw_away_from_fridge(item, trashcan, fridge)
                # Throw each item away

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior

behavior find_food_sugar_2070_around_fridge_140(food_sugar:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_sugar)
    body:
        assert is_food_sugar(food_sugar)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==140
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)
            exp(food_sugar,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_sugar,fridge_instance)

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_away_items_from_fridge(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            # For each item inside the fridge
            if inside(item, fridge):
                # Move the item into the trashcan
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior ensure_fridge_closed(fridge:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(fridge)
        # Ensure the fridge door is closed

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan

        throw_away_items_from_fridge(fridge, trashcan)
        ensure_fridge_closed(fridge)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior

behavior find_food_sugar_2070_around_fridge_140(food_sugar:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_sugar)
    body:
        assert is_food_sugar(food_sugar)

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_to_trashcan(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
            
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_items_to_trashcan(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end
